et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and the heat relieves the pain, just as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear for the patient who dies now, or a fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	Of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you cure the disease of the mouse according to what we have said about the divisions of cures, and it does not benefit, then there are three ways of cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of which one manner is that you make three cauterizations, or four, according to the length of the mouse, according to the figure of the liver caustic that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand all over the cauterization, and let the patient be aware of what's happening on their back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another manner of cauterization is that you scrape the caustic which has two edges, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the key that is near the mouse, or where the patient's skin comes towards the left side, and be the elevations which you lift with the key according to the key, according to the length of the body, and the cauterization should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After that, place the two edges inflamed so that the key is pierced from the other side, and then remove the cauterization, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see, then cauterize the entire fire cautery to three nurses.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the cure when he has got a purpuration by long time, and this is like the others of the cures said before.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery is not good for dropsy, unless it is done in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your cure does not benefit, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the mouth, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the kidneys, and two behind the back on the spine, and one in front of the breast.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterizations be well-nigh the spleen of good cheer.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open to allow purging for a long time, and do not cease the treatment of the patient after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would hasten, and the two intentions would be together with the aid of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly is the nail that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and he who has an olive-shaped back, according to what is mentioned here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the pines
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical and are full of yellowish pus, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the wrist bone and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery so as not to turn back.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too far in, thus the yellow water would burst forth, and the cauterize should be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Afterwards, make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the thumb bone;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauters be long, one under the knee in front and the other behind on the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauters open for a long time until the pus issues forth;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the healing of the other wounds that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a flux of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the vital and digestive forces that are in the stomach and intestine are weakened, and cannot be cured by methods of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient well suffering and of great virtue, so make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been said here before or stomach cauterization, to circulate cauterization.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four cauterizations around the mouth subtle for every cauterization is subtle, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the moisture abounding and the patient suffering, then make one cauterization on the navel, and one cauterization on each rib, and two small cauterizations on the stomach below the large one, because the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are in the fundament, one or more, and are ancient and are of thick cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit, so make cauterizations.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three on the back of the spine, that one which is entirely below the almond-shaped node and node in a triangular way, and one cauterization under the mouth two days.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is chilled and the meat does not cook, and one sees the face swell, then one makes a large cauterization on the stomach, as said before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen for all the subtle cauterizations.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment let it rest until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the swelling which is called "Thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut at the elbow, if the cautery appears to be red and raw, then put it all afire on the elbow that is being coped.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand stay there until the cautery comes to the birth of the vein, so that the blood does not cut.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is much elbow, then cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the cures of ointments, using them until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a great cautery on the head, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of an ill-cured wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or opening, as we will tell in its place, then comes this disease which cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When someone has a fistula, and it is inflamed and discharges foul-smelling pus and corrupted moisture, then you must carefully examine the entire tent (fold) to its deepest part.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After it appears red and raw, put the cautery in the fistula according to the quantity that the tumor has entered, and restart the cautery until the corrupt flesh is burned, once, or twice, or thrice, according to the quantity of the need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the nerve which are inflamed, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the bladder and intestine, then beware of these places, and do not make fires except in a well-enclosed space, and think that it is not a danger;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after the cure has been done as long as it is necessary, and if the wound is scaled over and the matter is removed after a long time, then you should know that the wound is entirely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter is not removed, know that the wound is putrid, and corrupts the bone to the foundation;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as one of those which we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	From the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain of cold comes to the ribs, and great windiness, and does not take shape like a woman, then it is necessary that you make a cautery on both sides of the ribs at the cauterized clave, as we have said before;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we were to cauterize it in the middle, there would be three cauterizations in a line, and they will provide greater help.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then one makes a cauterization on the part above the bladder, where the hairs of the scrotum begin, and there are two on the right side and two on the left side, and each should be as long as a nose's length.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and one makes another cauterization behind the back, where you have need of it;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and the cauterizations should be shaped like a key according to the form mentioned above.
de la marris	Of the womb
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the menses are cold and moist, and do not cease for this reason to conceive, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, it causes great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	Then it is necessary to make three fire cauterizations around the mouth, as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder, and two fire cauterizations behind the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauterizations be nail-shaped, as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the intestines
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends to the hollow of the hip, and because of this it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found that the navel is in the departing place of the abdomen, so it is necessary to cauterize the patient on the hollow of the hip with one cauterization resembling a circle, and sign before the navel around the hollow as it turns, so that the hollow be inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and let the cauterizations be such as those which we have cauterized on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, then do three cauteries of the olive-sized ones, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the keys.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and take care until he is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the intestines
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the groin of the hip, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is cured from what we have said in the section on boils, and the care does not work, and the illness is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the patient of the thick humors with foul pills or other good-smelling pills similar to these.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterward do a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cautery is according to two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	namely, hot medicines together, and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is according to many ways, of which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	That you cauterize on the back of the heel three triangular cauteries according to this form, and make a good depth and great, and have between each cautery a space the width of two fingers, and be the cauteries olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never has anyone done a cauterization in mid-heal on the top of the heel, because there are four according to this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, then make a cauterization at the circular cauterery that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the heel.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circle contains all the heel, and all the splinters of the nail are burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And it is the manner in which one does it in sciatica, when the pain holds in the thigh and does not reach as far as the hip or as far as the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the hip and leg, make two cauterizations on the side where the patient says that the pain holds him, and one above the ankle four finger widths to the left.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauterizing scalpel be, and let the thickness of the iron burn.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends up to two toes or almost to the knee, then he should cauterize where he feels the pain three points or four at the cautery which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	and if it is necessary, and it makes him even more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if he sees that the pain is under the knee towards the thigh, then make a cauterizing scalpel or circular one, and take good care in all your cauteries that you do not leave the cauterizer so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient more great discomfort and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have had a fire cautery on the ankle of the foot, and let them be until the leg was entirely swollen, and the feet also, and were pierced and corrupted all the feet.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a purgation of the belly from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two parts together, make a fire cautery on one and on the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men say in the cauterization of the groin, this is the manner: make it thus and be as thick at the head as a navillon of date, or a little less, and be between the interstices, and be from one interstice to another of the length of an elder's thumb.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the ligaments be like two parts, and also as if they were nails, and it has one band of iron well made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and let it be heated until it is entirely red and gives off sparks, and then put it on the boil of the patient's haunch, and let it turn on the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let the cauterizer do one fire once the cauterization is done, and let it leave for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make an ointment with butter, and let the wound remain open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of ointment until he is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use this fire cautery for the fear of its glance, and if we see not what is being used;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and yet these are good cauterizers, who can bear it, and where it affects.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of burning medicine is that you make an instrument with interstices where the edges of the door descend, and it be of earth or iron to a length of one span, and in its height have two notches, and between each notch the quantity of the thickness of a hen.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and be open on top and bottom, and join together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After put the handle of the haunch on the patient lying on a pig's side, and then place your hand above the handle of the haunch.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After pour the hot water between the two circles of the ewe that has been heated by fire in a pot, and let it stay for an hour or ten, and allow the patient to suffer from heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it also finds a cauterization like fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the ulcers are gone, raise your hand with the instrument and lift up the cloth of sweet oil, and let it be so for three days, and put on butter until what is black from scarring is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and leave it for three days that purulence may issue;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments as long as they are healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument hold oil according to what you have done in the correct manner;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the manner of hot oil, and I have written it or treated it as a chapter on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and hot water, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole so that the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put one pot on top of another well-weighted, and put on alum, charcoal, and sweet oil on top, until there are two layers above the powders then you will have it well prepared in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave him thus until he descends with an ague and fever or falls into a swoon, then take all that sweat and pour it on stones and on alkaline as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then if it will be much feverish and is administered in motion of works of medicine and in cauteries of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes an aching work like fire, and if there are other medicines which one cauterizes well on the skin thus as thesis, and honey mixed with anacardium and stones with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment by which one man was cured of the pain in his haunch and sciatic vein, and he greatly praised it, saying that no other treatment was done, and that he became well only once when this treatment was made, and he bathed himself just as he teaches below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And then in this manner you take green and fresh lardaric, and crush it much with a little bit of grease, and put it on the skin and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain holds, and bind it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours and by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed up, and then make him enter the bed, and the pain will go away entirely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery on such medicines unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dyscrates says that when the varicose vein is cauterized with goat's gall, it helps a lot.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and soak it in old oil, and place it on the hollow between the thumb of the foot and the other which is called a fleshy fold.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Then take dried goat's gall, and set it on fire until it becomes charcoal, and put it on the wool, and let it stay until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and do so again, and do not cease to do so until you think by sense that it will come up to the groin, and that the pain is ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this manner of cauterization is called "goat's gall cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	from the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or percussion or from too great evacuation, or from similar cold matter spread out, none of these likenesses is worth a cautery except for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after this that the patient be freed from fetid pills or similar things, and one should apply it to the back, there where the pain stays, three lines marked out, and in each line 5 cauteries or more according to virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let the cauterization be done according to the cauterization which is called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three cauterizations or four at the middle of the shoulder according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a thin, pale face when they wake up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find it in the lower back of the spine and on the appearance that comes over other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you wish to cure it, then cauterize at the "celcle" cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So the limb must be equally red throughout the cauterization.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spine with a fire cautery two or three lines away from each other, and have the points close to one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure, keep the wound so long as it is healing according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply cauterization in a hollow spot which is near a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	from the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of joints is from moisture that spreads to each member of the body, and when pain comes in feet, which doctors properly call "podagre", and when it is from a cold cause and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterizations in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make the majority of cauterizations around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterization be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need, then prick on the surface of the foot, so that the fire cautery claims "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, then make a fire cautery on each knee three or four times in each part, for all the olive-shaped cautery.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, then do it again, but don't keep your hand away from the fire's heat until the spark has burned out.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend as far as the knee and back, administer the fire cautery that we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make points around the knuckle two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains a point of pain on the fingers, then make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come to the shoulders or the back, then cauterize each part and take good care of the patient and administer medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make good governance and purge phlegm, he will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the roughness of the scurf.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When flux comes to the groin, and the bellies descend to the testicles and it is new, then it is necessary that when you see them cured, do not make him eat at all that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and he uses things that bring a stinking smell to his belly, so that the devil descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after he has sat on his back between your hands, and tells him to hold his elbow so that the swelling is repaired, and tighten them to your two arms, and draw down below the rash on the bone of the finger, and all in a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the fire cauterize which has this shape:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as he is white and gives signs.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then tighten the swellings to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the attendants hold his hand so that he does not return backward;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and work well the groins of the patient, and put underneath him the cushion and the servant on the groins, and another above the breast which holds his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the sign with your entire hand, and hold it straight and steady until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then continue again as many times as necessary to reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and watch carefully that the blister does not burst when you are doing the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you don't burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so the patient does not die or suffer another ill.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come close to the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that children's cauterizations be subtle according to their size, and for great people also great according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days' cure, apply the grease of butter to the site of the cautery until the scab is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the cure of other ointments until he is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for 40 days until the wound is well closed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nails are left to grow long, so that the bowels do not protrude when he will want to go into chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he will want to get up, let him be given a bandage well made, and wear it for 40 more days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him have good rest, that he does not labor too much and beware of too great drinking and eating, and too high bragging;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he has followed this instruction, then he is entirely well.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say next about the treatment of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	from the itch of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ulcers come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then make a fire cauterization on the cauterized part according to its size, and let it be burned to the third degree of heat;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the cure according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that one must cauterize at the fire cautery to three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but mark the first sign at the beginning and make a line on the width above the ulcer, and another below it, and draw your hand through all the cautery with a nail.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and moody.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any member, whether from falling or striking, and that pain lasts for a long time, and the cure of medicine is not worth it, then it is necessary that he be cauterized at the cautery which is called "poins", and the cauteries should be according to the length of the member, its smallness, weakness, and virtue, and its location of torments and pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is sound after the first cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	since then, start another cautery on top of that one; for it is custom that the member that is nearest should change, and therefore you must make the cauterizations until the patient is sound.
de meselerie	of surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The humors are helped sometimes by cautery with great help, and similarly the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can't you see it being cauterized, take heed if the patient is at the beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not spread nor remain, and you doubt that the corruption may overwhelm the entire patient, then make five cauterizations on top of the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I pierce to the forehead, and the other at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two above the two horns, and one behind above the haterel;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let your hand be so free that the fire comes to just above the bone, and as long as the scales come out so that the vapors of the great humors can come out;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize on the mouse according to what it is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the swelling is spread out everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is manifestly wasted, so you should apply the cauterizing of these fire cauterizations that we have said on the head, and one cautery on the nape, and two cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and six cauterizations on the spine of the back, and one great one on the coccyx and another nearby, and two above the two shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two above the sides, and two above the tendons of the breast, and one above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on the back lower leg, so you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes make a cauterization on the bone of the finger, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when I make more cauterization, it brings more help, and multiplies the benefit;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel pain from the cauterization as healthy people do, because the body is already all corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be great and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the manners of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the cure, wash the wound with flour mixed with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated by medications and oils and poultices, and it is not healed, then make cauterizations on the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be a little entering into the flesh of the quarter.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes one makes a cauterization at the hand and foot and back, at the issue of the nerve that moves the member, and thus if it is removed, the swelling remains.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and anyway no one intervenes unless they are knowledgeable about the members and the issues of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	of abscesses
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is inflamed, and the art of medicine is worthless, then cauterize it with a cautery deep enough, according to the quantity of the humor, until the swelling is removed, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then mix flour of vetches and lentils with rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood of hen and blood of crane, each in equal parts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and mix it all together, and bind it with a cloth, and apply it to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the cure for chancres by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre comes at the beginning, and you want to arrest it, so cauterize it with the cautery that seems like a circle, all around the perimeter of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And wise people say that one makes a fire cauterization also in the middle of the ulcer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and anyway it does not seem good to me, for I fear that it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen some times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more proper thing is that it be cauterized around, at the cauterization called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of inflammation that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it tarries to die or due to the superfluity that it makes or due to the age of the patient when he is decrepit (that is, too old) and he has little blood, or due to the weather;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it hastening to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize it around with many small cauterizations, piercing;
aprés le laisse ensi.	After that.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to kill.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing all the way through the entire cautery, then heat the cautery with whatever is on hand:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the midst of that disease which is called "adubelati" until the cauterizations have pierced the core, and be such cauterizations that the patient feels them outside in this manner as if the course of the disease were alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards cure him until he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cure for fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another manner of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing else than a wasting away of member, for it wastes away the members just as fire consumes dry straw.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can suffer from fire cautery together, then arrange the cauteries with small and great nails, according to what is needed at the location where the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	Afterward, cauterize all around until you have eradicated all corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and put on the cauterized areas a poultice made with oil as long as the burns of fire are removed, and all corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the ointment treatment has generated flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that sound flesh does not arise, then it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then recommence the cauterization on what remains of the corrupted flesh.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this remedy is sometimes used in place of fire cautery due to medicine's agreement in that location;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already said the cure for medicinal water in its division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take what you have need of.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of boils that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that on the feet by default a disease is born which is called "clos" according to our intention, and it is a large gap that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the fire cauterization of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	To know it is by fire cauterization and cauterization with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is such that you should heat the iron like a blacksmith's pen, and make it of good iron to the measure that it can pierce the nail from all sides, and have subtle margins.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After put all heat on the nail, and turn your hand entirely around the nail until it comes to the point of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	And leave it thus for three days until it begins to show purulence.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of wild mulberries pounded with oil, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall off and be detached from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the joint with oil, anointing it as much as is needed until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by outward signs on the body, and often occur in hands and feet, then it is necessary that you apply water cauterization.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in such a manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a brick of earth or iron, or a pin of wood, and place it on the nail and the other one, that is to say for small warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the brick on it so that it surrounds everything, then put a little bit of hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you go so that the edge of the brick comes to the root of the nail, and then the hot water can find its way deep down to the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little from the burning of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it so, and it will uproot itself entirely down to all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	So treat one after another, until you have reached all those within the body, then cure the humors which cause flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The cure of trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some shiver from cold or numbness, or from quartan fever or another, then it is necessary that you make him have 4 cauterizations or 5 on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and with fire cautery or weights, and on the stomach for olive oil cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	so let it shake, and hasten the health of the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of foul-smelling boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes appear on the outside of the body, or foul-smelling blisters, that come from great corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if necessary at first when they appear that one does fire cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle fire cautery of myrtle wood, by which the point is seized with fire, or a long Aristolochia root, or a lentil-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And whenever one cauterizes at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow forward anymore, but are broken off the superfluities from which they come, and are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often there occur great hemorrhages from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the afterdeath, or at the incision of an abscess, or at the cautery of a member, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very grievous thing to restrain.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet whenever this happens to someone, if you hasten to place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and strain it hard until the blood is calmed beneath your finger, and no more drips out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then set the olive oil cautery on fire with multiple small and large ones until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take one, either large or small according to the wound and the place where the artery is running, and put it on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery there until the blood is staunched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it bursts forth when you lift your fingers from the vein, and the cautery has cooled, then take quickly one other of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease to make those one after another until the blood is stopped.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you don't burn the nerve which is nearby, and that no other harm comes upon the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when a vein does not flow from the artery, one cannot well sustain oneself even when the artery is great, if it is not by one of the four ways that we have said:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or through burning, or by extracting it when not well treated, or by a strong bandage of thread, or by medicines placed on which have the power to constrict blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and be tied and steadied accordingly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the stanching of blood by binding tightly with cloths or putting burning things on, or similar things, unless it is not effective.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have a mirror or medicine present, then one should place the tip of their index finger on the wound in the vein as we said, and stretch it well until it is constricted above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move it, but moisten it with cold water often until it is very cold so that the blood is frozen and thickened and constricted.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries beforehand as to those things which he needs for cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	There begins the second book of surgical cures
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter all about every disease in which it is necessary to apply fire cautery or hot medicine, and the reasons, causes, and instruments of cauteries.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have put the first chapter at the beginning, and I will go on in this chapter by the same way, so that one may find more easily what one desires.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And thus, dear son, it is necessary that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for that reason it is necessary to be more cautious.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to take a foolish risk.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come into cures.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	Those who come from such people have so identified with their illness that they would die easily because of the desperation they find in their illness, and the magnitude of their wickedness.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And one should be afraid of these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And from those who give you their opinion and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not fitting that you agree with those who come to you who have this manner, but put more great caution in your honor than in your avarice, and do not foolishly but wisely from what you are certain of and can gain control of.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognostication and indication in the treatments of your illnesses, so that salvation may be converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and remembrance in praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, May Our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to be inspired by the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have concluded this chapter by dividing it into chapters, according to what is before the chapter on cauteries, which I have divided from the head to the end, so that you may find more easily what you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	of the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this sickness often comes to children during childbirth, and when the nurse holds the child's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from a known cause that one is unaware of.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this sickness except in children, and all the ones that I have seen died soon.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for that reason it seems to me that it is worth proceeding slowly with this work in such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw one child whose head was filled with water, and the head swelled each day until it could no longer be sustained.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture became so great that it was dead, and this moisture is gathered below the bone on top of the shoulder blade, between the vertebrae and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the work is such that if the moisture is between the vertebrae and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you cut a wide incision into the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it grow as long as two of us, until the moisture flows;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see to the form of the spatula-like thing;
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is below the bone, and you see signs that each part of the head has its commissures open, and when you press it with your hand from inside, the water jumps forth quickly, and this does not respond to you;
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	so it is necessary that you cut three incisions in the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After binding the incisions with cloths and powders, and applying wine and oil, and leaving it thus for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then loosen it, and treat the wound with tents and anointing, and let the head dry off, and then feed the patient dried meat mixed with moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another manner of incision is to look where the size of the abscess opens up, and the joining of water.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then where the abscess opens up, and the filling of water, and do what you can with it.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you don't cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and then comes forth blood, so that the patient may die from the loss of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of rheum (or discharge)
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to someone a disease called "catarre" in the eyes or at the liver, and the disease is old, and medical treatment does not help, then the last remedy is fire cauterization with which one will sear both arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary, when you see them cut open, that the patient make ready his head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the area with an asperous cloth until the arteries appear, then take away the patient's neck from the entire cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein beats, and the pulsations of one and the other are after the ears, and they are responded.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the pulses of both, then cut one and the other with a sharp knife two inches apart, as far as the vein reaches to the bone, and let it be by the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see, put the spatula under the artery and cut above it, cutting in two like a pair of scissors across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood will spring forth continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the touch, then it is necessary that you measure the quantity of space three fingers deep, then mark with an incision and cut to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and as much blood is to be let out if it is six ounces, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone point of the suprachondrium, then cut so that abscesses do not come there, then stop the wound and bind, and the treatment with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient migraine comes, and acute cataract, due to the moisture of tears and heat in temples and old forgotten habits and similar things, and he has been treated by methods of medical cures and all this does not benefit him, then we extract the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have recounted.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient makes sure the hairs on his temples are well-retracted, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, for it beats well and can be felt apart from some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is felt, the patient should loosen his neck with some cloths, then rub the area with a rough cloth, and rise up in hot water until the artery becomes manifestly apparent.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula whose shape is as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then grasp it at the top with tweezers, and part the veins that are below each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, then turn it to the point of the unguent, and cut off that part according to the quantity of the two veins.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For she is not cut, so does not flow all the blood at once.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And take out six cups of blood, down to three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, then it's necessary that you tie it in two loops with a strong double thread of silk, so that no bleeding occurs before the wound heals, and a decrease in blood comes.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then remove the excess that is between the two loops at the same hour, and then, if you see fit, apply the fire cautery with a cutlery knife just to the bone until the joints are cleared.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and that is the mother's work, if the patient does not have a fever and has a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterizing is helpful in finishing moles:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	therefore it is of greater help to moles.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Where it is necessary for the extraction of arteries that one fills the place with old cotton and puts on well-made tents.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when you loosen them, take care with dry medicines that bring forth flesh, and of poultices, until they are healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if there is no stoppage in the artery as long as you are working on it, then hasten to close with cautery, or use the location of vitriol and strain it to your hand that the blood be stopped.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you don't have that available, then put it on the wound so that the blood is frozen, and apply the location of cold water until the bleeding ceases, and strain it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and that which is more suitable and lighter in the extraction of the artery is to cauterize the vein with this cauterizing instrument cutting into two parts, but the cutting parts should be well spaced so as to withstand their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the cuttings are too dense, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be a large gap between the two knives, and then when you have signed off on the two holes, and you place the hot iron on top so that it comes just to the bone, and cut the vein into two parts.
