puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as with others that are torn open, so that no vessel bleeds which nourishes one of the testicles.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for in this case there is no harm coming from it, and if all the vessels come together, then it is necessary to draw out the testicles from all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the ears do not lose their nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they shrivel up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the roughness of the scurf.
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this remedy are by the section that comes from the hernia or the extension above the belly in the part of the groin, therefore the intestines descend into that hernia to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this hernia is either from the hernia or from the extension of it, and these two ways come from many causes.
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or by percussion, or by leap, or by braying, or by lifting a heavy burden, and through similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is of the extension due to syphilis, so it has poco and poco, in a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal up to the very bottom, because syphilis presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of the scurf, that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and there are diverse appearing abscesses below the skin near, and this is because of the issue of the intestine and the body flowing out of the scurf.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And at no time do the loops go down with the intestine, and are retained inside, and cause great suffering to the patient, especially when he is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron cures there is fear, why it must be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of the work is that you instruct the patient to put their hand inside the wound and into the intestines if they can fit.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then press down on his neck between your hands, and lift up the ribs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then stretch the skin above, and cut away all the skin of the scrotum long.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then put in the leaves of the size and shape that you need to open the wound, so that the eye may come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape off the white scurf that is below the skin of the testicles, until the white scurf is completely removed from all sides.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then press your thumb into the crease where the testicle is located, between the white scurf that is below the skin of the testicle and between the second scurf, and from behind the testicle, and between the second scurf.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then push with your right hand into the fold of the testicles, and lift the white scurf up to your left hand, and raise the testicle to all the scurf towards the waist.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to stretch the testicle up high, and release what is behind the tie;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask your hands if there is any point of the intestine enveloped or wrapped around the white scurf, and if you find anything, then push it into the belly underneath.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle where it has the thick thread made of ten threads, and bind it to the back part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the size, then cut the threads that appear from sons, as long as there are four threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then tie them one on top of the other in a cross-like manner, and bind the scrotum, which we have said is under the skin of the testicles, with a very strong cord of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the threads of sons around them, and tie them together with two parts, so that no vessels that nourish them can enter there, lest a suppurating abscess does not come to be;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and put the cord above that according to the first cord long two fingers of its length, and after these two cords leave the scrotum which is under the skin of the testicles a finger's width;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all other things according to the roundness that the egg bears;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part that is below the skin of the testicles, until the blood flows and the bowels move, as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wet wool in oil to wounds, and place on injuries, and apply the bandage that we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And any time the white sacrum bone is cauterized as we said, after incision, due to fear of excessive bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the bandage until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it does not fall off, then use hot water and apply to what we have said, until it falls off.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is healed perfectly.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshly hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this case I never saw anyone who dared to perform the treatment by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancient ones say that it is made like the tendril that surrounds the liver, in such a way that you bind the vessels, after cutting above and gently below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then strike me middle, and heal the abscess of those who work, until the servants die;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Once in a while comes gangrene in the fingers, as we have said, and opens up the flesh;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not remove any of the intestines from the abdomen, and if some come out, it is little, and repair them every hour;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and anyway if he stays too long in this position, the wound or abscess grows, until the intestines come out;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens through the extension of the abscess which is on the fingers, as we have said, because it is extended, then softened and swelled the flesh and opened up;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the cure is by cauterization, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is cured by fire in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and it is that the patient lies thus on his back between your hands, then shape the lump of swollen flesh to its natural size according to the quantity of three fingers.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then draw out the skin that is under the blister that follows, and take the red part and place it on top of the apparent flesh of the blister.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it to the bottom of the belly, then cut the two apparent blisters of the skin on top of the red part, and cut one and the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then draw out the top of the red part, and do not cut or stretch anything else, as I have shown you in the treatment of the hiccups of the intestines.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it by treating wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you dress the wounds, sooth and cure the sore, until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The sacrum is constricted, and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization is more effective in this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the coccyx
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the scrotum is softened in some men, because the things that are inside are softened, and it is to be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary when one wants to heal him that you make the patient lie down on his back and loosen the skin that is softened over natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then bring together the two lips at a seam, and if you see fit, sew up the excess of the softened skin at three seams or four firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then loosen between the seams and cover it as you would other wounds, until he is healed, and let the thread fall away.
dou chastrement	of punishment
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is esteemed in our law, and for this reason it would please me that I not speak of it at all in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary only by two means:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one of which is that the mirror responds in a healthy manner when one asks him about his health and about the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cattle and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is done in two manners:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by traction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In that which we do by traction, we make the beast sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and relaxed.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them with your hand, until they are relaxed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of castration by size:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you bind the beast and press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut on each testicle one stroke, when you have well circumcised them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave no part of the scrotum or the thin scrotal sac that is above the vas deferens;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this manner of castration is more sure than that which is done by traction, because in the traction something may remain of the testicles by chance, whereby the beast desires lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then cure the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermafrodite is according to two manners in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one being that between the two testicles it opens like the shape of a woman's nature, or he has hair, and sometimes in court his urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has above the elbow as a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the care for men and women is that you cover all the sores together, and care for them just as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, of men whose urine jumps through the skin of the testicles, there is no care.
de la tentigene	Of tetinegine
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigo is a sore located on the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it just as large as a hand, and that's the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You should dye the excess of the tentigo on your hand or on nails, and cover it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep into it, lest bleeding ensues, then treat with another treatment until they are healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and at another sign that appears on the lips of the mouth, and the swelling, and by chance jumps forth, and is according to the likeness of a cow, and for this reason the ancient people called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you cut it, as we have said the incision, and cure until it is healed.
de erratique	Of erratic
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	it is erroneous when the woman's natural state is not perceived, or the pustule is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is a natural occurrence by birth, or an accident caused by disease that has come into being;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is due to a festering sore, or subtle or sharp abscess, and it occurs in the mouth, or on the sides, or below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and hinders conception, and childbirth, and by chance the flowers of having children;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of this is by the observation of the bale.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the swelling appears close to appearing, it is at your breasts or in the armpit.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is a boil that is subtle and it is close to two books, then hasten and read thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two index fingers together, and the woman be on her back, spread her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then place the two books firmly, until the subtle boil is resolved, and cover it with poultices;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and soak it in oil, and put it on the boil, and place the woman at home each day, so that she cannot coagulate.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the abscess is hard and thick, so it is necessary that you cut it with a spatula resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the poultice is of new charcoal, then suspend it on a hook and cut it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stopping medicines, such as aloe, dragon's blood, and aloeswood, together with abundant egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then provide a strap of linen wide enough so that the wound cannot heal.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and thus be long, and provide a cloth of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then be treated with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when in the marshes there comes flesh born, so it is necessary to cut it according to this manner, unless it be enchanted abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For the enchanted abscess in the marsh, one must not touch with fire.
des emorroides	Of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Varices are openings of veins that are not accustomed to being cut, and when varices are old they become hardened.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have said in the division the likenesses of them, and the signs, and I will say now those that receive cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and piles, when they are deeply seated in the anus, and do not sense pain, are not cured by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the entrance of the anus, where one can feel them, are those that one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Then it is necessary that you put the woman in a cold house, then take away the swelling with tweezers, and chop off its roots, then powder on medicines that restrain blood, such as aconite and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then bind her feet with a bandage for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	et if bleeding occurs from it comes let the poultice sit on a decoction of sumac and orange peel and galls and similar things then take barley flour and mix with honey and oil and make an application on his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if he stays still, it's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping glasses to the back and breast so they don't cause pain.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take linen, moisten it in plantain juice or agrimony juice with old wine, and apply to the place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has healed, then treat the joint with ointment until it is sound.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles the gouty joint, so it must be covered as I said earlier.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat it until it is sound.
des apostemes de la marris	Of apostemes of the belly
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many kinds of abscesses come to the marriage, such as chancre and bony abscess and herpes and boils and blisters and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have said in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is necessary then that I say in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes in marriage, which is not one of the abscesses that cools down.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the work of iron, then observe whether the abscess is angry at the beginning of its arrival, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red so that you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then don't hurry to puncture, but let it cool down until the pain is appeased.
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a stool, and have two small stools or he reclines, and lean back on his back and bring his feet to the opposite side of the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his hips be spread apart, and put his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good cord.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then the ball goes towards the right side, and one brings in the instrument with which one works at the mouth of the mare's, from which the form comes.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you bring in this instrument, you make the first mark on it so as to know the depth of the mare's, so that what enters into the instrument does not go too far and does not hurt the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the mare's with cloths, so that the instrument does not cause her distress.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he puts the bell of the instrument above and holds the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens and one does it gently with the hand, then it is necessary to cover it at the top, at the spatula-like place.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowstring is empty, so it is necessary that you put damp linen cloths soaked in rose oil or green oil in the wound;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the cloth far from the wound at the bottom of the bed, and place it above the bed and on the clean linen cloth moistened in water or mulberry leaves that are cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then the patient after two days of dressing, according to this, until they are healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and at any time lift the bed and the wound by rinsing with water and honey, and then with water or lily roots and aloe long cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to dressing.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is covered with a marsh, then it is necessary to take care not to cook anything made of iron, but rather care for it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first at the bedside that she knows the shape of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman go down below, and desire to give birth.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	Then the child hastens to come out quickly;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	Then you know that this childhood is according to natural form, and the exit is under its head, and the second one with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to press gently on his belly, so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he descends above his head, the afterbirth comes with him, and the mother is rid of her excesses through good purging;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this one that comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it comes sometimes on his feet, and comes forth from the body or from the head, or hands, or comes above his belly, or in some other way, and is turned by chance around his neck, and through other bad forms;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	so it is necessary for the bailiff to be wise and subtle in these things, and wary of error and deception, and I will show you all the forms how one should help him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes onto its head by natural birth, and the mother gives birth with difficulty, and the baby's strength is weak, then make it sit on a stool or have women hold it.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And let the baby's natural excretion of oil or fenugreek be cooked, and then pour it between its navel and the little space that is the form.
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and cut the scab, and scrape off the nail as much as the moistors that are in the wound can do it.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and paint the woman's belly as long as the baby descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to purge the woman with fenugreek mixture with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her take a condiment and sternutate, and keep her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if it stays now the baby.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands are far apart, you must pull them together gently little by little;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, then the woman sits on the seat and lifts up her feet high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then put the stool on the ground, and hold the woman so she does not stumble while standing up;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot enter and the child is dead, then cut the hands with the knife that was placed here before, extract the child, and pull them together evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes onto its feet, you should support it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take the foot and stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the hips, then command it to bend, and make it stretch again with condiments;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps away, may God will.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not further than we have said, then turn it bit by bit until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be easier.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it doesn't come away as we have said, take myrrh of aloes, and oil of sassafras, and melted gum, and grind everything in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put it on the nature of the woman inside and pour this unguent down to her navel, then make her sit in cold water down to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened underneath, make a poultice of myrrh and put it underneath and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make her sit on a stool, then make her walk and restrain her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child is now jumping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the exit of the child from its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, I put the bail of its hands pinch by pinch;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	Then be mindful of his neck, and let his feet hang down below, and let him rest on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and fold his hands little by little, and then take hold of his hands on the belly, and remove the pillows underneath, until it is arranged below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the infant does not jump, then take his feet and shape them well, then shape the belly upwards, then put your hands in.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and stroke the child gently.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to take hold until the infant comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the exit of the child that comes out with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to contrive how to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot bring it back, then make the woman get up and go;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then make her lie on the bed, and take off her legs well.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then administer the musculage that I have recounted;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not abort, then make her sit on the siege, then study how to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and shape it according to natural form, and make her stretch out, and command her to take hold until the child comes forth.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the exit of the child from its neck, and having spread out its hands, and its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	it is necessary that the midwife holds onto her hand, then turns it back and forth, and gently guides;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, then put on the natural musculage of oil and aloes, as we have said, then command her to move back and forth;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, then make her sit on the siege, and command her to take hold;
et la fai esternuer.	and make her stretch out.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same manner for all the intestines
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes forth in this manner to the entire second stage, then cut the afterbirth with your finger, until the fluids are emptied;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child bites its face and neck, then cut off the lips so they are not retained, and kill the child.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then wrap the child in it until you have put it as it should be, and instruct the woman to take care of herself sometimes:
adonques si istra legierement.	then if it starts to loosen slightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	From the exit of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes four at once;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are a strange thing, and do not live unless one can name them;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply, and are torn apart by the womb which devours them, which is bound to the lips;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out naturally as one would expect, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are bruised, then do the treatment as we have said, and the doctor should be skillful, and make soon and lightly what he makes;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do so that it may be for the salvation of the patient.
de plusors enfans	Of multiple children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Certain times are formed in the months I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or even up to XV, and they are all shaped like an infant by the measurement of sage glory; and it is necessary that the doctor knows everything, because by chance similar things happen to him.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	and do as is fitting.
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman after a dead or stillborn child, as I said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to do manual work;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	so that you know whether the woman is of good virtue, and has no accident or fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary that the woman sits upright on her back, and has her knees inclined downward, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply a poultice to the woman's back in two parts, or she be bound to bed so that she is not troubled by the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then smear the mouth of the mare with moist oils mixed with alti and fenugreek and flaxseed, then anoint the bail's hands with these oils and these mixtures;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then put them in the mare lightly, then take up or down as she puts on or off what is suitable to those things, and be careful if the child appears prepared to descend onto its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the cord presents in her eyes or in her neck or mouth or palate or below the beard or in the throat or near the ribs, and if the descent is on the feet, then take hold or pinch it and adjust the sides accordingly;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	et covient qu'il tiengne l'oncine à sa main dextre, et mette la corbeure entre ses doigts de la sinestre main, et le boute à tout sa main légerement, et fiché l'oncine en aucun de ces lieux que nous avons dit, tant qu'il vienne à la chose vide;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and that is the shape of the tool:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then place it opposite another tool, or the third one if you need it, so that the extractions be equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it equally by moving from one side to the other, so that the tools fit together, and the tool's teeth hold them in place, as is its form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if there remains a part, then oil the nail of some of its fingers with oil, and grease that part, and draw out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if there's no more of it, so put this cone or higher up, and do it until he gets out all the way.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other, and he cannot bring it back due to constriction, so you should wrap it on top with a cloth until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	then bind at the joint of the foot or at the heel, and thus it is necessary that you do the same in the other hand, and with two feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the child is large and it is narrow in the exit, or it has a sharp point assembled, so you should put the spatula-shaped spine between your thighs, and make the head and extract the liquid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you shape it with the instrument called "almidach", from which the form comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus likewise makes itself naturally great of head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with pincers, and if the head jumps out and it is held by the forceps, so that it is split, until the moisture which is in the wound is pulled out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces to whatever extent you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, then it is necessary that you make a hole until the moisture runs.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is gentle, and the direction to the mouth of the mother is gentle.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is strained in the belly or chest, then it is necessary that you extract it with a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and make an incision in the belly or chest until the moisture which is there runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is removed, and the head remains, then thrust your hand into the depth of the wound, and pull it up to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then I apply one needle or two, and train him/her;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed because of an abscess that has come, then it is not necessary to work at all, but rather it is necessary to apply moist and greasy things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the applier applies ointments, and such things in water that are softening and moistening.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can put it equal, then apply what we have said to a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot do that, then train him/her by parts, and leave nothing of the secondary.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if the applier applies what we have said to abscesses that come in the wound;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding comes from the wound, then it should be put in restraining water, and the applier should apply other remedies.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose child in her womb had been dead, then she consulted another on top of it, and refused the dead one.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came forth in her mouth and swelled so much that it burst open, and caused great turmoil.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the treatment, and I thought for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied ointment of strong attraction, and one bone came out, and after a few days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	So I thought that it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I sought the wound and treated it with many bones, until the woman was in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman stayed like that for a long time, and thereupon a little pus came from it.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I do not remember this chapter except for the reason that, when a master finds a strange thing, he should know how to help it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	on restoring the mother to her place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Thereafter comes the form of the pressor, by which we use books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns to the two joints of the two ligaments.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the combs should be more subtle than the restrainer, and should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the beam should be one foot and a half in width, and the edge of the trees, one palm and a half long.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two ligaments there should be two gashes of the same beam, which are tight in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are fitted together in the mouth of the mare to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, resembling it in subtlety and lightness, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the appearance of pincers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two joints, just like you see, one palm in length and two digits in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see to open the mare entirely with all the instrument, make the woman sit on it, her feet pendant and legs outstretched, then put the two joints together in the mare, and hold the head of the instrument beneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the entire instrument, just like you have done with pincers evenly, according to the quantity that you see opening the mouth of the mare, until it does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all topped, and their likenesses are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the mirrors are prepared, then the work is done more quickly, and it is more suitable for people according to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despise the instrument that you have not prepared, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the secondine is retained at childbirth, then it is necessary to instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then have her exhale slowly, and hold your hands on her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she struggles for that reason, well it is.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, then I take a pot and make a perforation or covering, and put in herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as chamomile, rue, anise, camomile, casaline and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, being cooked or put in water above the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put a cord or pipe of the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the mother, and tie it so that the fumes come inside the mother;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then let her vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the secondine starts to move quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and is not well, instruct the nurse to moisten her left hand with sesame oil or with muskadel from elderberry, and then pour it into her natural place, and make her rinse again.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take hold of it and stretch it slowly and steadily so that the mother does not resist the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it is necessary to move it slightly to the right and to the left, and then pull;
si venra et se desaerdra.	so it will come out and be dislodged.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the mother is obstructed, we have said the remedy for vomiting, and fumigation with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if she is not from all that we have said, so guard that you do not stray away.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that what is at the mouth of the marriage, you bind to the woman's hip, then anoint her with four-drug ointment.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	so she will recover and be put back together, and will come forth.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nonetheless, when she recovers thus comes forth a bad smell from the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So it is necessary to make suitable fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	none of the ancients have tried fumigation with cabbage and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumes the woman at the retention of flowers and secondine is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it looks like a chain, and you put the headpiece subtle in its natural state, and the large nails above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and make the fumigations above the coals, and let the itching continue until it is worn out, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Some children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but it is stopped by subtle osseous fibers.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So then it is necessary for the needle to pierce that osseous fiber at its proper point, and not to penetrate excessively deep, and to guard the location so it does not touch.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put on a moist linen cloth in wine and oil, then an ointment treatment until he is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not close, then put in a perforation a piece of cloth, and leave it for many days, and be removed when the child wants to go to chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this stoppage occurs suddenly from a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	So then it is necessary to cover that stoppage:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	So he is cured, as we have said about the caustic.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from under the foundation are nodulation, and grow larger than those that come from above the foundation or in the space between two parts, whether one or more fistulas.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that swelling is old, it works, and with added moisture becomes white or subtle bluish, and sometimes these boils burst;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and are followed by what comes out or is ejected through urine or flatulence when the patient has bowel movement, and sometimes jumps up accidentally.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if the boils burst just to the bladder, and just to the middle of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach just to the junction of the hip, and just to nothing of the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the boil bursts at the fundament, and does not burst:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you thrust your index finger or fundament, and thrust a thin needle of iron or steel into the boil when there is no twistiness.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twistiness, then you thrust a thin linen cloth or a horsehair into the boil as far as you can feel the cloth or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you don't feel it, and it doesn't come with defecation or vomiting or fever, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not break through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to heal.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula persists just to the bladder or just to the urethral conduit of urine, then the urine jumps out and cannot be healed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced just to the joint of the hip, then the tendons come up to the place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the origin of the pain around it, then it is that he goes away slowly, and it is not worth medicine nor soothing by anointing;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these Persian fistulas there is no cure other than hard work, and vanity of foolish physicians who meddle with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In one that is not Persian and is not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have tried, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient lifts his legs down to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then pitch a tent of earth, or of cloth if there is twistiness, until you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around his foundation, then you should put your two fingers there, and if he senses then that the tent has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and when it is discovered where you feel between your finger and the flesh or skin, then know that it is pierced.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not intervene there, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says however that some can be healed, but this is rare;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid one gives there is to cauterize the ulcer subtlety according to the width of the abscess, as was said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and warm the poultice thoroughly in the fistula, until it reaches the foundation;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that these burnt remnants are like a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat with moist tents in butter, until the burnt remnants issue forth, and then treat with ointment, binding and sealing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healed, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If that, in no other way, cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent is inserted and does not penetrate all the way to the docket which is at the foundation, and there is a thick covering of char or pus between your shoulder and the tent, and you see the fistula opening up where the covering meets the flesh;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	so scrape off the beginning of the fistula and insert it before the tent, and then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be freed the tent, and falls;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then remove those charred hairs that appear like a bird's feather, and leave none remaining.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood swells up and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or medicine again.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery brings together two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	namely, the burning away of these charred hairs, and the stopping of blood and the drying up of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat damp tents with butter or crushed charcoal, until the wound drips pus, and issue forth the burned hairs in the pus;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of scabby flesh that forms hard scales, and are the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes right through to the fundament and is distant from the body, then place your thumb or fundament on it and investigate this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent and between two is the flesh or the scab or char, when it is close to piercing, unless there are fires that go by way of faith and hope, through the administration of one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	You cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it down to the bone, or if you can, place tents and care for it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	And don't go too far in depth, lest you cut the dwelling that holds the foundation, and the evacuations come forth without intention.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then care for it, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is clean, or you remove that covering and then wash it since it has been cut beneath the foundation, or by tent or other appointed instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse that foul flesh which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound and to keep the fistula in the part beyond the foundation:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And no fistulas are formed in this way:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you set up the tent in the abscess, and it is on the outside of the foundation beneath the skin above, so take a piece of cloth with a perforation at the top according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I wrap one thread twisted in two, and wrap the poultice all around the thread in the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced on the edge of the foundation inside, then pull out the thread from that perforation, so that you set up your tent or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and draw the top of the thread, and tie the two ends together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it so that the thread cuts through the flesh between the two, and discharges.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is closed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not perforate, then make it perforate in all the ways that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it does not behoove to cut open too deeply in the first instance, and then heal, as we have said, until he is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spatula-like spine that one makes for the abscess is much rougher on one side and cut away.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand no, because one does not strike what one must not strike, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Wounds are according to two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	or they are within the foundation, like a kernel of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in short time blood flows, and there is one or more, and they go below the foundation and at the top of the foundation;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are below have little moisture, and in short time or a little of yellowish water or a little blood, and they have the color of flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them within the foundation is that you instruct the patient to sit down in a chamber until the foundations come forth, and then the sons appear;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you hurry, and pinch it with pincers, or hold it to your nail, then strike at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the ligaments cannot hold them due to their moisture, so they take to drapery, or to cloth, or to a piece of camlet;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them to your hands, then cut, and powder with some hot powders that are in place of a cauterizer;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as it is said or written in the chapter on cauterization, then cure with other cures until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, so you purge the patient with a biting and harsh purgative to clean what is in the foundation, so that it may come out openly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	if the patient takes offense, and if the thread is too far from the foundation, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and that you grasp them with your finger or with forceps, and cut, then cure as we have said, until he is healed, and so that he does not fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You must bring together the stitching according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, and put it into an awl, then draw the thread above and make the awl pierce on the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread below the awl, so that they be of equal width.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and strain the thread tightly, then knot the thread, and pull out the awl, and do so with all the others, and let only a small amount of excess blood remain.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then put on the foundation a moist cloth soaked in rose oil or cerot, and put on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him be until he has voided, and when they are done, treat him with ointment and other treatments, until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of the burning of the skin or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times happens burning of the skin in the intestine, and by constraint of nature, and when the patient is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must reset to the tip of a spatula or your fingernail's skin above, which does not let it get moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then cure it until it is solid as it is necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot dry, then repeat the scraping more strongly than before, until it heals slowly and is scraped off;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cure it until it is healed.
dou fremit	of the tremble
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Fomice is a small appearance of an abscess near the body, and goes very deep inside;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it bursts and becomes frosty, and one feels it just like a dead feeling of numbness, and spreads throughout the body, and more so in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure is to take a cord made of goose quill or strong oxen hair, and put that cord on the numbness, until the circles purple the numbness entirely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all the cordage until you coil it all around the trembling part, and put it in deep, and shake out the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, then make it of a needle or iron according to this form, and be subtle underneath and drawing above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, but rather hold steady at two [points], and press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, then cauterize the trembling part, just as it is shown in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	One never makes a poultice of silver or archwood, or of melted or powdered tin;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and one never makes any of these small and great instruments according to the manner in which they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those then which are used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, whether small or great, is as follows: the belly is tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and if there is a deviation or the bowels are bound, as you see, and the head inside is pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and has two holes on one side and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	et be the belly where one puts medicines from a beast's bladder or parchment, and be pierced all around with small holes, and have between each hole as much space as I should deserve, then put into these holes a strong thread of green silk twisted in X or in a circle, and tie up the belly so that it is like a goat.
